      size=3>主要内容<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 2">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 6.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=10 width="6%" noWrap>
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>1<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 12.32%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=10 width="12%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>《党政机关厉行节约反对浪费条例》中发<SPAN lang=EN-US>[2013]13</SPAN>号<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第八条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>党政机关应当遵循先有预算、后有支出的原则，严格执行预算，严禁超预算或者无预算安排支出，严禁虚列支出、转移或者套取预算资金。年度预算执行中不予追加，因特殊需要确需追加的，由财政部门审核后按程序报批。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 3">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十一条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>全面实行公务卡制度。健全公务卡强制结算目录，党政机关国内发生的公务差旅费、公务接待费、公务用车购置及运行费、会议费、培训费等经费支出，<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 4">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十三条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>党政机关应当建立健全并严格执行国内差旅内部审批制度，从严控制国内差旅人数和天数，严禁无明确公务目的的差旅活动，严禁以公务差旅为名变相旅游，严禁异地部门间无实质内容的学习交流和考察调研。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 5">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十六条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>外事管理部门应当加强因公临时出国审核审批管理，对违反规定、不适合成行的团组予以调整或者取消。无出国经费预算安排的不予批准，确有特殊需要的，按规定程序报批。严禁违反规定使用出国经费预算以外资金作为出国经费，严禁向所属单位、企业、我国驻外机构等摊派或者转嫁出国费用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 6">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>党政机关应当建立公务接待审批控制制度，对无公函的公务活动不予接待，严禁将非公务活动纳入接待范围。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 7">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建立国内公务接待清单制度，如实反映接待对象、公务活动、接待费用等情况。接待清单作为财务报销的凭证之一并接受审计。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 8">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十七条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>公务用车实行政府集中采购，应当选用国产汽车，优先选用新能源汽车。公务用车保险、维修、加油等实行政府采购，降低运行成本。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 9">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第三十条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>党政机关会议实行分类管理、分级审批。财政部门应当会同机关事务管理等部门制定本级党政机关会议费管理办法，从严控制会议数量、会期和参会人员规模。完善并严格执行严禁党政机关到风景名胜区开会制度规定。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 40.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 10">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 40.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第三十二条 建立健全培训审批制度，严格控制培训数量、时间、规模，严禁以培训名义召开会议。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 11">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">严格执行分类培训经费开支标准，严格控制培训经费支出范围，严禁在培训经费中列支公务接待费、会议费等与培训无关的任何费用。严禁以培训名义进行公款宴请、公款旅游活动。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 71.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 12">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 6.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=4 width="6%" noWrap>
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>2<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 12.32%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=4 width="12%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>《机关事务管理条例》国务院令 第<SPAN lang=EN-US>621</SPAN>号<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十二条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>应当根据工作需要和机关运行经费预算制定公务接待费、公务用车购置和运行费、因公出国（境）费支出计划，不得挪用其他预算资金用于公务接待、公务用车购置和运行或者因公出国（境）。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 42pt; mso-yfti-irow: 13">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 42pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十三条　不得出租、出借办公用房或者改变办公用房使用功能；未经本级人民政府批准，不得租用办公用房。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 71.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 14">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十五条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>应当建立健全公务用车配备更新管理制度，不得超编制、超标准配备公务用车或者超标准租用车辆，不得为公务用车增加高档配置或者豪华内饰，不得借用、占用下级单位和其他单位的车辆，不得接受企业事业单位和个人捐赠的车辆。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 52.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 15">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 52.3pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十六条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>应当对公务用车实行集中管理、统一调度，并建立健全公务用车使用登记和统计报告制度。政府各部门应当对公务用车的油耗和维修保养费用实行单车核算。 
      <SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 62.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 16">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 6.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=4 width="6%" noWrap>
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>3<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 12.32%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=4 width="12%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>《党政机关国内公务接待管理规定》<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第七条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>无公函的公务活动和来访人员一律不予接待。公务活动结束后，接待单位应当如实填写接待清单，并由相关负责人审签。接待清单包括接待对象的单位、姓名、职务和公务活动项目、时间、场所、费用等内容。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 71.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 17">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>确因工作需要，接待单位可以安排工作餐一次，并严格控制陪餐人数。接待对象在<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>10</SPAN>人以内的，陪餐人数不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>人；超过<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>10</SPAN>人的，不得超过接待对象人数的三分之一。工作餐应当供应家常菜，不得提供鱼翅、燕窝等高档菜肴和用野生保护动物制作的菜肴，不得提供香烟和高档酒水，不得使用私人会所、高消费餐饮场所。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 71.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 18">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十二条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>禁止在接待费中列支应当由接待对象承担的差旅、会议、培训等费用，禁止以举办会议、培训为名列支、转移、隐匿接待费开支；禁止向下级单位及其他单位、企业、个人转嫁接待费用，禁止在非税收入中坐支接待费用；禁止借公务接待名义列支其他支出。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 62.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 19">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十四条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>接待费报销凭证应当包括财务票据、派出单位公函和接待清单。接待费资金支付应当严格按照国库集中支付制度和公务卡管理有关规定执行。具备条件的地方应当采用银行转账或者公务卡方式结算，不得以现金方式支付。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 63.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">未经批准或授权，不得对外发出正式邀请或作出承诺。接待计划应当明确外宾团组中由我方招待的人数、天数，费用开支范围以及资金来源、列支渠道、预算等。计划编制必须严格控制在年度外宾接待费预算内，不得突破。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 42.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 21">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 42.3pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">外宾接待费的报销支付应严格按照国库集中支付和公务卡管理的有关制度执行，采用银行转账或公务卡方式结算，不得以现金方式支付。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 49.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 22">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 49.3pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第九条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">外宾接待经费开支范围主要包括：住宿费、日常伙食费、宴请费、交通费、赠礼等。外宾接待经费原则上不得列支外宾来华国际旅费。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27.35pt; mso-yfti-irow: 23">
    <TD

  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.8pt; mso-yfti-irow: 24">
    <TD

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">（二）外宾宴请费（含酒水、饮料）标准：正、副部长级人员出面举办的宴会，每人每次<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>400</SPAN>元；司局级及以下人员出面举办的宴会，每人每次<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>300</SPAN>元。冷餐、酒会、茶会分别为每人每次<SPAN lang=EN-US>150</SPAN>元、<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>100</SPAN>元、<SPAN lang=EN-US>60</SPAN>元。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 41.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 25">

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">（三）外宾在华期间，宴请不得超过<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>次，包含赴地方访问时，由地方接待单位或有关单位联合安排的<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>次宴请。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>

      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN

      lang=EN-US>400</SPAN>元；赠礼方或受礼方为司局级人员的，每人次礼品不得超过<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>200</SPAN>元；其他人员，可以视情况赠送小纪念品。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>

      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>（二）应急保障用车和其他按照规定配备的公务用车配备价格<SPAN lang=EN-US>18</SPAN>万元以内、排气量<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>1.8</SPAN>升（含）以下的轿车或者其他小型客车。确因情况特殊，可以适当配备价格<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>25</SPAN>万元以内、排气量<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>3.0</SPAN>升（含）以下的其他小型客车、中型客车或者价格<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>45</SPAN>万元以内的大型客车。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 73.1pt; mso-yfti-irow: 31">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 73.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>（三）执法执勤用车配备价格<SPAN lang=EN-US>12</SPAN>万元以内、排气量<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>1.6</SPAN>升（含）以下的轿车或者其他小型客车，因工作需要可以配备价格<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>18</SPAN>万元以内、排气量<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>1.8</SPAN>升（含）以下的轿车或者其他小型客车。确因情况特殊，可以适当配备价格<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>25</SPAN>万元以内、排气量<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>3.0</SPAN>升（含）以下的其他小型客车、中型客车或者价格<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>45</SPAN>万元以内的大型客车。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 32">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>（四）特种专业技术用车配备标准由有关部门会同财政部门按照保障工作需要、厉行节约的原则确定。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 29.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 33">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><SPAN

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公务用车配备新能源轿车的，价格不得超过<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>18</SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 62.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 34">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十五条　除涉及国家安全、侦查办案等有保密要求的特殊工作用车外，党政机关公务用车产权注册登记所有人应当为本机关法人，不得将公务用车登记在下属单位、企业或者个人名下。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      size=3>第十六条　严禁公车私用、私车公养，不得既领取公务交通补贴又违规使用公务用车。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

      size=3>第十九条　应当建立公务用车管理台账，加强相关证照档案的保存和管理。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

      size=3>第二十条　应当建立健全公务用车使用管理制度，严格执行，加强监督，降低运行成本。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>

      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

      size=3>第九条　中央垂直管理部门所属单位的一般公务用车、执法执勤用车、特种专业技术用车和其他用车配备更新计划，由各主管部门负责编制。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 42.65pt; mso-yfti-irow: 43">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 42.65pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      size=3>第十七条　公务用车运行费用包括公务用车燃料费、维修费、保险费、过路过桥费、停车费和其他相关支出。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56pt; mso-yfti-irow: 44">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十一条　公务用车预算下达后，各部门、各单位应当严格执行，原则上不予调整。因特殊情况确需调整的，应当按照规定程序报经财政部门审批。资金支付按财政国库管理制度有关规定执行。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

    <TD

      size=3>《因公临时出国经费管理办法》<SPAN 
    lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 53.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第六条 
      因公临时出国经费的支付，应当严格按照国库集中支付制度和公务卡管理制度的有关规定执行。严禁接受或变相接受企事业单位资助，严禁向同级机关、下级机关、下属单位、企业、驻外机构等摊派或转嫁出访费用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 62.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 46">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 62.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第七条各单位应当建立因公临时出国计划与财务管理的内部控制制度。出访团组应当事先填报《因公临时出国任务和预算审批意见表》，由单位外事和财务部门分别出具审签意见，明确审核责任。出国任务、出国经费预算未通过审核的，不得安排出访团组。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 54pt; mso-yfti-irow: 47">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 54pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第八条 
      因公临时出国经费包括：国际旅费、国外城市间交通费、住宿费、伙食费、公杂费和其他费用。公杂费是指出国人员在国外期间的市内交通、邮电、办公用品、必要的小费等费用。其他费用主要是指出国签证费用、必需的保险费用、防疫费用、国际会议注册费用等。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 54pt; mso-yfti-irow: 48">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 54pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第九条 
      （三）因公临时出国购买机票，须经本单位外事和财务部门审批同意。机票款由本单位通过公务卡、银行转账方式支付，不得以现金支付。单位财务部门应当根据《航空运输电子客票行程单》等有效票据注明的金额予以报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 57.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 49">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 57.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十条 
      出国人员根据出访任务需要在一个国家城市间往来，应当事先在出国计划中列明，并报本单位外事和财务部门批准。未列入出国计划、未经本单位外事和财务部门批准的，不得在国外城市间往来。出国人员的旅程必须按照批准的计划执行，其城市间交通费凭有效原始票据据实报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 54pt; mso-yfti-irow: 50">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 54pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十三条 
      出访团组对外原则上不搞宴请，确需宴请的，应当连同出国计划一并报批，宴请标准按照所在国家一人一天的伙食费标准掌握。出访团组与我国驻外使领馆等外交机构和其他中资机构、企业之间一律不得用公款相互宴请。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 51">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十四条 
      出访团组在国外期间，收授礼品应当严格按有关规定执行。原则上不对外赠送礼品，确有必要赠送的，应当事先报经本单位外事和财务部门审批同意，选择具有民族特色的纪念品、传统手工艺品和实用物品。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 54pt; mso-yfti-irow: 52">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 54pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十五条 
      出国签证费用、防疫费用、国际会议注册费用等凭有效原始票据据实报销。根据到访国要求，出国人员必须购买保险的，应当事先报经本单位外事和财务部门批准后，按照到访国驻华使领馆要求购买，凭有效原始票据据实报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 39pt; mso-yfti-irow: 53">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 39pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十六条 
      出国人员回国报销费用时，须凭有效票据填报有团组负责人审核签字的国外费用报销单（具体表格由各单位制定）。各种报销凭证须用中文注明开支内容、日期、数量、金额等，并由经办人签字。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 17.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 54">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 17.3pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><SPAN 
      style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">各单位财务部门应当根据本办法制定本单位财务报销审批的具体规定，加强对因公临时出国团组的经费核销管理。对因公临时出国团组提交的出国任务批件、护照（包括签证和出入境记录）复印件及有效费用明细票据进行认真审核，严格按照批准的出国团组人员、天数、路线、经费预算及开支标准核销经费，不得核销与出访任务无关的开支。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 38.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 55">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 38.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 6.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=15 width="6%" noWrap>
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>8<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 38.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 12.32%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=15 width="12%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>《中央和国家机关会议费管理办法》<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 38.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第五条　各单位应当严格会议费预算管理<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>控制会议费预算规模。会议费预算应当细化到具体会议项目<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>执行中不得突破。会议费应当纳入部门预算<SPAN lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>并单独列示。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 71.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 56">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 71.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第七条　中央和国家机关会议按以下程序和要求进行审批<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>:</SPAN>三类会议。各单位应当建立会议计划编报和审批制度<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>年度会议计划<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>(</SPAN>包括会议数量、会议名称、召开的理由、主要内容、时间地点、代表人数、工作人员数、所需经费及列支渠道等<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>)</SPAN>经单位领导办公会或党组<SPAN lang=EN-US>(</SPAN>党委<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>)</SPAN>会审批后执行。四类会议。由单位分管领导审核后列入单位年度会议计划。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 57">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>年度会议计划一经批准<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>原则上不得调整。对党中央、国务院交办等确需临时增加的会议<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>按规定程序报批。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 58">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第八条　二、三、四类会议会期均不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>天<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>;</SPAN>传达、布置类会议会期不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>天。会议报到和离开时间<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>一、二、三类会议合计不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>天<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>四类会议合计不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>天。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 59">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第九条　各单位应当严格控制会议规模。三类会议参会人员不得超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>150</SPAN>人<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>其中<SPAN lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>工作人员控制在会议代表人数的<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>以内。四类会议参会人员视内容而定<SPAN lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>一般不得超过<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>50</SPAN>人。<SPAN 
    lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 60">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十三条　参会人员以在京单位为主的会议不得到京外召开。各单位不得到党中央、国务院明令禁止的风景名胜区召开会议。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 51pt; mso-yfti-irow: 61">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 51pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十四条　会议费开支范围包括会议住宿费、伙食费、会议场地租金、交通费、文件印刷费、医药费等。交通费是指用于会议代表接送站<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>以及会议统一组织的代表考察、调研等发生的交通支出。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 62">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十五条　会议费开支实行综合定额控制<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>各项费用之间可以调剂使用。综合定额标准是会议费开支的上限。各单位应在综合定额标准以内结算报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 63">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十六条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN>二、三、四类会议费原则上在部门预算公用经费中列支。会议费由会议召开单位承担<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>不得向参会人员收取<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>不得以任何方式向下属机构、企事业单位、地方转嫁或摊派。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 69.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 64">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 69.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十七条 
      各单位在会议结束后应当及时办理报销手续。会议费报销时应当提供会议审批文件、会议通知及实际参会人员签到表、定点会议场所等会议服务单位提供的费用原始明细单据、电子结算单等凭证。财务部门要严格按规定审核会议费开支<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>对未列入年度会议计划<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>以及超范围、超标准开支的经费不予报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 65">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十八条 各单位会议费支付<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>应当严格按照国库集中支付制度和公务卡管理制度的有关规定执行<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>以银行转账或公务卡方式结算<SPAN lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>禁止以现金方式结算。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 21pt; mso-yfti-irow: 66">

      size=3>第二十五条 各单位的主要职责是<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 17.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 67">
    <TD

      lang=EN-US>)</SPAN>负责制定本单位会议费管理的实施细则<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 17.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 68">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 17.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>)</SPAN>负责单位年度会议计划编制和三类、四类会议的审批管理<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 69">
    <TD

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>)</SPAN>负责安排会议预算并按规定管理、使用会议费<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>做好相应的财务管理和会计核算工作<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>对内部会议费报销进行审核把关<SPAN lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>确保票据来源合法<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>,</SPAN>内容真实、完整、合规<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>

      size=3>央和国家机关差旅费管理办法<SPAN 
    lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 63.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal

      size=3>第七条　出差人员应当按规定等级乘坐交通工具。部级及相当职务人员出差，因工作需要，随行一人可乘坐同等级交通工具。未按规定等级乘坐交通工具的，超支部分由个人自理。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 71">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第十条　乘坐飞机、火车、轮船等交通工具的，每人次可以购买交通意外保险一份。所在单位统一购买交通意外保险的，不再重复购买。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 72">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      size=3>第十三条　部级及相当职务人员住普通套间，司局级及以下人员住单间或标准间。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27pt; mso-yfti-irow: 73">
    <TD

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      size=3>第十六条　伙食补助费按出差自然（日历）天数计算，按规定标准包干使用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 29.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 74">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal

      size=3>第二十条　市内交通费按出差自然（日历）天数计算，每人每天<SPAN lang=EN-US>80</SPAN>元包干使用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 37.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 75">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 37.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      size=3>第二十三条　城市间交通费按乘坐交通工具的等级凭据报销，订票费、经批准发生的签转或退票费、交通意外保险费凭据报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 48.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 76">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 48.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>　　住宿费在标准限额之内凭发票据实报销。伙食补助费按出差目的地的标准报销，在途期间的伙食补助费按当天最后到达目的地的标准报销。市内交通费按规定标准报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 43.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 77">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 43.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十四条　工作人员出差结束后应当及时办理报销手续。差旅费报销时应当提供出差审批单、机票、车票、住宿费发票等凭证。住宿费、机票支出等按规定用公务卡结算。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 57.1pt; mso-yfti-irow: 78">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 57.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十五条　财务部门应当严格按规定审核差旅费开支，对未经批准出差以及超范围、超标准开支的费用不予报销。实际发生住宿而无住宿费发票的，不得报销住宿费以及城市间交通费、伙食补助费和市内交通费。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 77.8pt; mso-yfti-irow: 79">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 77.8pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第二十六条　各单位应当加强对本单位工作人员出差活动和经费报销的内控管理，对本单位出差审批制度、差旅费预算及规模控制负责，相关领导、财务人员等对差旅费报销进行审核把关，确保票据来源合法，内容真实完整、合规。对未经批准擅自出差、不按规定开支和报销差旅费的人员进行严肃处理。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 56.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 80">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 56.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>第三十条　工作人员外出参加会议、培训，举办单位统一安排食宿的，会议、培训期间的食宿费和市内交通费由会议、培训举办单位按规定统一开支；往返会议、培训地点的差旅费由所在单位按照规定报销。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 69pt; mso-yfti-irow: 81">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 69pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 6.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=10 width="6%" noWrap>
      <P class=MsoNormal

      align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>10<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 69pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 12.32%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    rowSpan=10 width="12%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><FONT 
      size=3>《中央和国家机关培训费管理办法》<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 69pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建立培训计划编报和审批制度。各单位培训主管部门制订的本单位年度培训计划（包括培训名称、目的、对象、内容、时间、地点、参训人数、所需经费及列支渠道等），经单位财务部门审核后，报单位领导办公会议或党组（党委）会议批准后施行。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 36.05pt; mso-yfti-irow: 82">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 36.05pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">各单位年度培训计划于每年<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>月<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>31</SPAN>日前同时报中央组织部、财政部、国家公务员局备案。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 46.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 83">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 46.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第八条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">本办法所称培训费，是指各单位开展培训直接发生的各项费用支出，包括师资费、住宿费、伙食费、培训场地费、培训资料费、交通费以及其他费用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 45.05pt; mso-yfti-irow: 84">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 45.05pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第九条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">除师资费外，培训费实行分类综合定额标准，分项核定、总额控制，各项费用之间可以调剂使用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27.3pt; mso-yfti-irow: 85">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27.3pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">师资费在综合定额标准外单独核算。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 31.45pt; mso-yfti-irow: 86">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.45pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">组织培训的工作人员控制在参训人员数量的<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US>10%</SPAN>以内，最多不超过<SPAN lang=EN-US>10</SPAN>人。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 24.35pt; mso-yfti-irow: 87">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 24.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十五条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">邀请境外师资讲课，须严格按照有关外事管理规定，履行审批手续。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 66.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 88">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 66.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">报销培训费，综合定额范围内的，应当提供培训计划审批文件、培训通知、实际参训人员签到表以及培训机构出具的收款票据、费用明细等凭证；师资费范围内的，应当提供讲课费签收单或合同，异地授课的城市间交通费、住宿费、伙食费按照差旅费报销办法提供相关凭据。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 32.05pt; mso-yfti-irow: 89">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 32.05pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width="81%">
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan" 
      align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十九条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">培训费由培训举办单位承担，不得向参训人员收取任何费用。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.65pt; mso-yfti-irow: 90; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.65pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 81.34%; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"

      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十四条</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">各单位可以按照本办法，结合本单位业务特点和工作实际，制定培训费管理具体规定。<SPAN 
      lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE>
